         L     R1,0(R1)               POINT TO PARM                     00085
         CLC   0(2,R1),=H'0'          Q. ANY PARM                       00086
         BE    STCK                   A. NO                             00087
         CLC   2(6,R1),=C'TESTIT'     Q. IS PARM TESTIT                 00088
         BNE   STCK                   A. YES                            00089
         SPACE 1                                                        00090
         MVI   TESTIT+1,X'00'         SET TEST SWITCH                   00091
         LA    R10,0                  FORCE 1ST ENTRY                   00092
         LA    R12,MLTBL              POINT TO 1ST MSG ADDR             00093
         B     SETPTR                                                   00094
STCK     STCK  DWORD                                                    00095
         SR    R10,R10                                                  00096
         ICM   R11,7,DWORD+2          GET PART OF CLOCK                 00097
         LA    R11,0(R11)             PURIFY IT                         00098
         SPACE 1                                                        00099
         D     R10,=A((ML00000-MLTBL)/4)  DIVIDE BY NUMBER OF ENTRIES   00100
         SLL   R10,2                  MULT REMAINDER BY 4               00101
SETPTR   LA    R9,MLTBL(R10)          POINT TO MSG ADDRESS              00102
         L     R8,0(R9)               GET THE MSG ADDRESS               00103
         LA    R7,75                  STD MSG LENGTH                    00104
         B     TPUTLOOK                                                 00105
TPUTLOOK CLI   0(R8),X'FE'            Q. ANY MSG TO PUT OUT             00106
         BE    TESTIT                 A. NO                             00107
         PRINT  GEN                                                     00108
         TPUT  (R8),(R7),R                                              00109
         AR    R8,R7                  INDEX TO NEXT LINE                00110
         B     TPUTLOOK                                                 00111
TESTIT   B     ENDIT                                                    00112
         LA    R12,4(R12)                                               00113
         C     R12,=A(ML00000)        Q. END OF MSG LIST                00114
         BE    ENDIT                  A. YES                            00115
         LA    R10,4(R10)             BUMP INDEX                        00116
         LR    R1,R10                                                   00117
         SRL   R1,2                   DIVIDE BY 4                       00118
         CVD   R1,DWORD               MAKE IT PACKED                    00119
         UNPK  WORK,DWORD                                               00120
         OI    WORK+4,X'F0'           REMOVE SIGN                       00121
         TPUT  MSG#,L'MSG#                                              00122
         B     SETPTR                 AND LOOP                          00123
ENDIT    EQU   *                                                        00124
RETURN  EQU  *                                                          00125

*                                                                     * 01741
*  RULES:                                                             * 01742
*    1) DOUBLE QUOTES (") CAN BE USED AT ANY TIME IN THE TEXT         * 01743
*    2) IF A SINGLE QUOTE (') IS USED IN THE TEXT THEN YOU MUST       * 01744
*       USE TWO SINGLE QUOTES ('') TO GET ONE QUOTE.                  * 01745
*    3) NO MORE THAN 75 CHARACTERS CAN BE DISPLAYED ON A LINE.        * 01746
*    4) USE MASK1 AND MASK2 FOR POSITIONING.                          * 01747
*                                                                     * 01748
*                                                                     * 01749
* MASK1    ....+....1....+....2....+....3....+....4....+....5....+....6 01750
* MASK2        ....+....7....+                                          01751
*********************************************************************** 01752
